[30;1m24 | [0m[35m    changelog[0m
[30;1m25 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m26 | [0m[35m``versioningit`` is yet another Python packaging plugin for automatically[0m
[30;1m27 | [0m[35mdetermining your package's version based on your version control repository's[0m
[30;1m28 | [0m[35mtags.  Unlike others, it allows easy customization of the version format and[0m
[30;1m29 | [0m[35meven lets you easily override the separate functions used for version[0m
[30;1m30 | [0m[35mextraction & calculation.[0m

[30;1m71 | [0m[35mdetermining your package's version based on your version control repository's[0m
[30;1m72 | [0m[35mtags.  Unlike others, it allows easy customization of the version format and[0m
[30;1m73 | [0m[35meven lets you easily override the separate functions used for version[0m
[30;1m74 | [0m[35mextraction & calculation.[0m

[30;1m33 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m34 | [0m[35m``versioningit`` is yet another Python packaging plugin for automatically[0m
[30;1m35 | [0m[35mdetermining your package's version based on your version control repository's[0m

[30;1m39 | [0m[35m``versioningit`` follows `Semantic Versioning`_, in which the major version[0m
[30;1m40 | [0m[35mcomponent is incremented whenever a breaking change is made.  Moreover, the[0m
[30;1m41 | [0m[35mbasic ``pyproject.toml`` interface to ``versioningit`` can be considered very[0m
[30;1m42 | [0m[35mstable; the only changes to expect to it will be the addition of new features[0m
[30;1m43 | [0m[35mand the occasional patching over of corner-case bugs.  Nearly all breaking[0m
[30;1m44 | [0m[35mchanges will be to the library or custom method API; if you've written any code[0m
[30;1m45 | [0m[35mthat uses this part of the API, you are advised to declare the next major[0m
